class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%84%9F%E6%9F%93%E7%A7%91&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="感染科（页面不存在）">感染科</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Infectious_disease_(medical_specialty)" title="en:Infectious disease (medical specialty)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Infectious disease (medical specialty)</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%B8%E8%85%94%E9%86%AB%E5%AD%B8" title="胸腔醫學">胸腔醫學</a></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>肺炎</b>（<span lang="en">pneumonia</span>），是指<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E9%83%A8" title="肺部">肺部</a>出現<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%99%BC%E7%82%8E" title="發炎">發炎</a>的症狀，主要是<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E6%B3%A1" title="肺泡">肺泡</a>受到影響<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RespText09_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-RespText09-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AcuteCare09_13-0"><a href="#cite_note-AcuteCare09-13">[13]</a></sup>。肺炎常見的症狀包括有<a href="/wiki/%E7%97%B0" title="痰">痰</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%92%B3%E5%97%BD" title="咳嗽">咳嗽</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%B8%E7%97%9B" title="胸痛">胸痛</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%99%BC%E7%86%B1" title="發熱">發熱</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E5%9B%B0%E9%9A%BE" title="呼吸困难">呼吸困難</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ash2007_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-Ash2007-2">[2]</a></sup>。症狀可能由輕微到嚴重不一<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIH2011_14-0"><a href="#cite_note-NIH2011-14">[14]</a></sup>。特別高齡的長者或新生兒可能會出現不典型的症狀<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup>。通常在治療開始後三天會逐漸好轉；然而，患者在未來一個月以上可能會感到疲倦<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIH2011_14-1"><a href="#cite_note-NIH2011-14">[14]</a></sup>。
</p><p>肺炎通常是受到<a href="/wiki/%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="病毒">病毒</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%8F%8C" title="細菌">細菌</a>感染而引發的，偶爾會由其他<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="微生物">微生物</a>感染引起。另外<a href="/wiki/%E8%97%A5%E5%93%81" title="藥品">藥品</a>影響或者是<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E9%AB%94%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E6%80%A7%E7%96%BE%E7%97%85" title="自體免疫性疾病">自體免疫性疾病</a>也會造成肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RespText09_4-2"><a href="#cite_note-RespText09-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jeff2010_5-1"><a href="#cite_note-Jeff2010-5">[5]</a></sup>。危險因子包括諸如<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%8A%E8%85%AB%E6%80%A7%E7%BA%96%E7%B6%AD%E5%8C%96" title="囊腫性纖維化">囊腫性纖維化</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%85%A2%E6%80%A7%E9%98%BB%E5%A1%9E%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%97%85" title="慢性阻塞性肺病">慢性阻塞性肺病</a>的肺部疾病，以及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B0%A3%E5%96%98" title="氣喘">氣喘</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%B3%96%E5%B0%BF%E7%97%85" title="糖尿病">糖尿病</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%BF%83%E8%87%9F%E8%A1%B0%E7%AB%AD" title="心臟衰竭">心臟衰竭</a>、具<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%B8%E8%8F%B8" title="吸菸">吸菸</a>史，還有使咳嗽能力貧弱的<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E9%A2%A8" title="中風">中風</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E6%8A%91%E5%88%B6" title="免疫抑制">免疫抑制</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup>。肺炎往往是根據症狀以及<a href="/wiki/%E7%90%86%E5%AD%B8%E6%AA%A2%E6%9F%A5" title="理學檢查">理學檢查</a>來判斷。<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%B8%E9%83%A8X%E5%85%89" title="胸部X光">胸部X光</a>、血液測試，<a href="/wiki/%E7%97%B0" title="痰">痰</a>液<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Microbial_culture" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="微生物培養"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%9F%B9%E9%A4%8A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="微生物培養（页面不存在）">微生物培養</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microbial_culture" title="en:Microbial culture"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Microbial_culture</span></a></span>）</span></span>都能幫助確認診斷<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIH2011Diag_7-1"><a href="#cite_note-NIH2011Diag-7">[7]</a></sup>。這個疾病可以依照感染的地點分類為社區、醫院、或醫護相關的肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup>。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E7%96%AB%E8%8B%97" title="疫苗">疫苗</a>可用於防止特定種類的肺炎，其他預防包含多<a href="/wiki/%E6%B4%97%E6%89%8B" title="洗手">洗手</a>和禁菸<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIH2011Pre_9-1"><a href="#cite_note-NIH2011Pre-9">[9]</a></sup>。治療方式則取決於造成疾病的根本原因<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIH2011_14-2"><a href="#cite_note-NIH2011-14">[14]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%97%E7%BB%86%E8%8F%8C%E8%8D%AF" title="抗细菌药">抗生素</a>可用於治療細菌造成的肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIH2011Tx_10-1"><a href="#cite_note-NIH2011Tx-10">[10]</a></sup>，如果病人病情嚴重，通常會住院治療<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIH2011_14-3"><a href="#cite_note-NIH2011-14">[14]</a></sup>。當病人氧氣含量低時，會用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B0%A7%E6%B0%A3%E6%B2%BB%E7%99%82" title="氧氣治療">氧氣治療</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NIH2011Tx_10-2"><a href="#cite_note-NIH2011Tx-10">[10]</a></sup>。
</p><p>全球每年約有4.5億人（全球人口的7%）罹患肺炎，每年約400萬人因此死亡<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lancet11_11-3"><a href="#cite_note-Lancet11-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CochraneTx13_12-2"><a href="#cite_note-CochraneTx13-12">[12]</a></sup>。肺炎被十九世紀時的醫生<a href="/wiki/%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E5%A5%A5%E6%96%AF%E5%8B%92" title="威廉·奥斯勒">威廉·奧斯勒</a>視為「死亡統帥」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup>。在二十世紀，抗體和疫苗的發明使存活率得以改善<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lancet11_11-4"><a href="#cite_note-Lancet11-11">[11]</a></sup>。然而，開發中國家居民、年老、年幼與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%85%A2%E6%80%A7%E7%96%BE%E7%97%85" title="慢性疾病">慢性疾病</a>患者，肺炎依然高居<a href="/wiki/2002%E5%B9%B4%E8%87%B4%E6%AD%BB%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E5%8F%8A%E6%89%80%E5%8D%A0%E6%AF%94%E4%BE%8B%E5%88%97%E8%A1%A8" title="2002年致死原因及所占比例列表">主要死因之一</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lancet11_11-5"><a href="#cite_note-Lancet11-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup>。由於肺炎經常縮短垂死之人的煎熬，因此被稱為「老人之友」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EBMED05_20-0"><a href="#cite_note-EBMED05-20">[20]</a></sup>。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E7.97.85.E5.BE.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="病徵">病徵</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：病徵">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table align="right" class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="2">症狀及發生比率<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tint10_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-Tint10-21">[21]</a></sup>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th>症狀</th>
<th>發生比率
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td>咳嗽</td>
<td><center>79–91%</center>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>疲勞</td>
<td><center>90%</center>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>發燒</td>
<td><center>71–75%</center>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>呼吸困難</td>
<td><center>67–75%</center>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>多痰</td>
<td><center>60–65%</center>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>胸痛</td>
<td><center>39–49%</center>
</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Symptoms_of_pneumonia.svg"><img alt="肺炎主要症狀的人體示意圖" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1045" data-file-width="1055" decoding="async" height="297" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Symptoms_of_pneumonia.svg/300px-Symptoms_of_pneumonia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Symptoms_of_pneumonia.svg/450px-Symptoms_of_pneumonia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Symptoms_of_pneumonia.svg/600px-Symptoms_of_pneumonia.svg.png 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Symptoms_of_pneumonia.svg" title="放大"></a></div>感染性肺炎的主要症狀</div></div></div>
<p>感染性肺炎的症狀有<a href="/wiki/%E5%92%B3%E5%97%BD" title="咳嗽">咳嗽</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%99%BC%E7%87%92" title="發燒">發燒</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E7%99%BC%E5%86%B7" title="發冷">發冷</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E5%9B%B0%E9%9A%BE" title="呼吸困难">呼吸困難</a>，深呼吸時會<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%B8%E7%97%9B" title="胸痛">胸痛</a>，而且<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Respiratory rate" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="呼吸率"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="呼吸率（页面不存在）">呼吸率</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Respiratory_rate" title="en:Respiratory rate"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Respiratory rate</span></a></span>）</span></span>較高<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BMJ06_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-BMJ06-8">[8]</a></sup>。年長者最明顯的症狀是意識不清、心智的變化或混亂<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BMJ06_8-2"><a href="#cite_note-BMJ06-8">[8]</a></sup>。五歲以下兒童的典型症狀是發燒、咳嗽及呼吸困難<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup>。
</p><p>小於五歲小孩的症狀則包含發燒、咳嗽、呼吸困難或呼吸加快<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-1"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup>。但發燒不只是肺炎的症狀，也是許多疾病常見的症狀，而且在重病或<a href="/wiki/%E7%87%9F%E9%A4%8A%E4%B8%8D%E8%89%AF" title="營養不良">營養不良</a>的情形下可能不會出現。而不足兩個月大的兒童若得到肺炎，一般不會有咳嗽的症狀<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-2"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup>。其他兒童身上更嚴重的症狀有<a href="/wiki/%E7%99%BC%E7%B4%BA" title="發紺">皮膚發紫</a>、不想喝水、抽搐、持續嘔吐、發高燒或是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Altered level of consciousness" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="意識水平下降"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%84%8F%E8%AD%98%E6%B0%B4%E5%B9%B3%E4%B8%8B%E9%99%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="意識水平下降（页面不存在）">意識水平下降</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Altered_level_of_consciousness" title="en:Altered level of consciousness"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Altered level of consciousness</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-3"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-0"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。
</p><p>細菌性和病毒性肺炎通常症狀類似<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WHOPrevent2012_25-0"><a href="#cite_note-WHOPrevent2012-25">[25]</a></sup>，部分引起肺炎的病原常發生某些非特異性症狀，但具有這些症狀的患者並不能確診為該病原引起。例如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%80%80%E4%BC%8D%E8%BB%8D%E4%BA%BA%E8%8F%8C" title="退伍軍人菌">退伍軍人菌</a>引起的肺炎可能伴隨腹痛、腹瀉或迷亂發生<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup>；<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E9%8F%88%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="肺炎鏈球菌">肺炎鏈球菌</a>引起的肺炎則可能帶有鏽色的痰液，而<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E9%9B%B7%E4%BC%AF%E6%B0%8F%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E8%8F%8C" title="克雷伯氏肺炎菌">克雷伯氏肺炎菌</a>所引發的肺炎則可能產生類似「黑醋栗果凍」的血痰。但<a href="/wiki/%E5%92%B3%E8%A1%80" title="咳血">血痰</a>並不是肺炎特有的症狀，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%B5%90%E6%A0%B8" title="肺結核">肺結核</a>、革蘭氏陰性菌肺炎、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="lung abscess" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="肺膿瘍"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E8%86%BF%E7%98%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="肺膿瘍（页面不存在）">肺膿瘍</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/lung_abscess" title="en:lung abscess"><span dir="auto" lang="en">lung abscess</span></a></span>）</span></span>，以及<a href="/wiki/%E6%80%A5%E6%80%A7%E6%94%AF%E6%B0%A3%E7%AE%A1%E7%82%8E" title="急性支氣管炎">急性支氣管炎</a>等皆會發生<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup>。黴漿菌性肺炎可能和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Cervical lymphadenopathy" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="頸部淋巴腺病變"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%A0%B8%E9%83%A8%E6%B7%8B%E5%B7%B4%E8%85%BA%E7%97%85%E8%AE%8A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="頸部淋巴腺病變（页面不存在）">頸部淋巴腺病變</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cervical_lymphadenopathy" title="en:Cervical lymphadenopathy"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Cervical lymphadenopathy</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%B3%E8%8A%82%E7%97%9B" title="关节痛">關節痛</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E8%80%B3%E7%82%8E" title="中耳炎">中耳炎</a>有關<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-1"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。病毒性肺炎比細菌性肺炎更常伴隨<a href="/wiki/%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E6%80%A5%E4%BF%83" title="呼吸急促">呼吸急促</a>的發生<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WHOPrevent2012_25-1"><a href="#cite_note-WHOPrevent2012-25">[25]</a></sup>。過去相信類似症狀應該是由類似的原因所引起，因此分類成「典型」及「非典型」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M32_28-0"><a href="#cite_note-M32-28">[28]</a></sup>。然而，證據並不支持這項分類方式，因此這個分類法不再受到重視<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M32_28-1"><a href="#cite_note-M32-28">[28]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E8.87.B4.E7.97.85.E5.8E.9F.E5.9B.A0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="致病原因">致病原因</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：致病原因">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Streptococcus_pneumoniae.jpg"><img alt="Three one round objects in a black background" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="488" data-file-width="700" decoding="async" height="153" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Streptococcus_pneumoniae.jpg/220px-Streptococcus_pneumoniae.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Streptococcus_pneumoniae.jpg/330px-Streptococcus_pneumoniae.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Streptococcus_pneumoniae.jpg/440px-Streptococcus_pneumoniae.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Streptococcus_pneumoniae.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AD%90%E9%A1%AF%E5%BE%AE%E9%8F%A1" title="電子顯微鏡">電子顯微鏡</a>下的<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E9%8F%88%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="肺炎鏈球菌">肺炎鏈球菌</a>（<i>Streptococcus pneumoniae</i>），為一種常見的肺炎病原體</div></div></div>
<p>肺炎的致病原因以<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%8F%8C" title="細菌">細菌</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="病毒">病毒</a>為主，偶爾是由<a href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C" title="真菌">真菌</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%84%E7%94%9F%E8%99%AB" title="寄生虫">寄生蟲</a>引起。雖然目前有超過一百株的致病原被鑒別出來，當中卻只有幾株是確定會真正造成主要感染原因的。病毒與細菌的交叉感染的機率大約是，幼童45%，成人15%<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lancet11_11-6"><a href="#cite_note-Lancet11-11">[11]</a></sup>。即使仔細地檢測，能夠被鑑定出來的確診感染原大約只有一半而已<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EBMED05_20-1"><a href="#cite_note-EBMED05-20">[20]</a></sup>。
</p><p>肺炎（英語：<span lang="en">Pneumonia</span>）有時會更廣泛地用於所有的肺部發炎，比如起因於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E9%AB%94%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E7%96%BE%E7%97%85" title="自體免疫疾病">自體免疫疾病</a>、化學灼傷、藥物反應等非感染因素，然而這種發炎應稱為非感染性肺炎（英語：<span lang="en">Pneumonitis</span>）（中譯亦簡稱肺炎）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-isbn0-7234-3200-7_29-0"><a href="#cite_note-isbn0-7234-3200-7-29">[29]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup>。
</p><p>導致肺炎的環境及風險因子包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%8A%BD%E8%8F%B8" title="抽菸">抽菸</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E9%AB%94%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E7%BC%BA%E4%B9%8F" title="自體免疫缺乏">自體免疫缺乏</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%85%92%E7%B2%BE%E4%B8%AD%E6%AF%92" title="酒精中毒">酒精中毒</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%85%A2%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E9%83%A8%E9%98%BB%E5%A1%9E%E7%96%BE%E7%97%85" title="慢性肺部阻塞疾病">慢性肺部阻塞疾病</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%93%AE%E5%96%98" title="哮喘">哮喘</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%85%A2%E6%80%A7%E8%85%8E%E8%87%9F%E7%96%BE%E7%97%85" title="慢性腎臟疾病">慢性腎臟疾病</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%9D%E7%97%85" title="肝病">肝病</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-2"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup>。酸抑制療法的應用（像是<a href="/wiki/%E6%B0%AB%E9%9B%A2%E5%AD%90%E5%B9%AB%E6%B5%A6%E9%98%BB%E6%96%B7%E5%8A%91" title="氫離子幫浦阻斷劑">氫離子幫浦阻斷劑</a>或<a href="/wiki/H2%E5%8F%97%E4%BD%93%E9%98%BB%E6%8A%97%E5%89%82" title="H2受体阻抗剂">H2受体阻抗剂</a>）也與肺炎風險上升相關<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup>，風險會隨年齡增長而升高<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-3"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.B4.B0.E8.8F.8C"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="細菌">細菌</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：細菌">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%8F%8C%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E" title="細菌性肺炎">細菌性肺炎</a></div>
<p>細菌感染是造成<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Community-acquired pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="社區性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A4%BE%E5%8D%80%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="社區性肺炎（页面不存在）">社區性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Community-acquired_pneumonia" title="en:Community-acquired pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Community-acquired pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>的主要原因，有將近50%的案例都可以分離出<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E9%8F%88%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="肺炎鏈球菌">肺炎鏈球菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-0"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EOP10_34-0"><a href="#cite_note-EOP10-34">[34]</a></sup>，其他可以分離出的細菌有20%的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%81%E6%84%9F%E5%97%9C%E8%A1%80%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="流感嗜血桿菌">流感嗜血桿菌</a>、13%的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Chlamydia pneumoniae" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="肺炎衣原菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E8%A1%A3%E5%8E%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="肺炎衣原菌（页面不存在）">肺炎衣原菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chlamydia_pneumoniae" title="en:Chlamydia pneumoniae"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Chlamydia pneumoniae</span></a></span>）</span></span>，3%的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E5%88%86%E6%9E%9D%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="肺炎分枝桿菌">肺炎分枝桿菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-1"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup>，其他的還有<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%91%E9%BB%83%E8%89%B2%E8%91%A1%E8%90%84%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="金黃色葡萄球菌">金黃色葡萄球菌</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Moraxella catarrhalis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="卡他莫拉菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%A1%E4%BB%96%E8%8E%AB%E6%8B%89%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="卡他莫拉菌（页面不存在）">卡他莫拉菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moraxella_catarrhalis" title="en:Moraxella catarrhalis"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Moraxella catarrhalis</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%97%9C%E8%82%BA%E5%86%9B%E5%9B%A2%E8%8F%8C" title="嗜肺军团菌">嗜肺军团菌</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%A9%E5%85%B0%E6%B0%8F%E9%98%B4%E6%80%A7%E8%8F%8C" title="革兰氏阴性菌">革兰氏阴性桿菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EBMED05_20-2"><a href="#cite_note-EBMED05-20">[20]</a></sup>。上述病菌中有許多已出現有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%80%90%E8%8D%AF%E6%80%A7" title="耐药性">耐药性</a>的菌種，例如耐药肺炎链球菌（DRSP）及<a href="/wiki/%E8%80%90%E7%94%B2%E6%B0%A7%E8%A5%BF%E6%9E%97%E9%87%91%E9%BB%84%E8%89%B2%E8%91%A1%E8%90%84%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="耐甲氧西林金黄色葡萄球菌">耐甲氧西林金黄色葡萄球菌</a>（MRSA）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-4"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。
</p><p>當有一些容易造成肺炎的危險因子時，細菌就有可在生物體傳播的途徑<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EBMED05_20-3"><a href="#cite_note-EBMED05-20">[20]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E9%85%97%E9%85%92" title="酗酒">酗酒</a>和肺炎鏈球菌、<a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%AD%E6%B0%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="厭氧生物">厭氧生物</a>及肺炎分枝桿菌的感染有關，抽煙則容易造成肺炎鏈球菌、流感嗜血杆菌、卡他莫拉菌和嗜肺军团菌的感染，接觸鳥類和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Chlamydia psittaci" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="鹦鹉热衣原体"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%B9%A6%E9%B9%89%E7%83%AD%E8%A1%A3%E5%8E%9F%E4%BD%93&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="鹦鹉热衣原体（页面不存在）">鹦鹉热衣原体</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chlamydia_psittaci" title="en:Chlamydia psittaci"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Chlamydia psittaci</span></a></span>）</span></span>有關，農場動物和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Coxiella burnetti" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="贝氏柯克斯体"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%9D%E6%B0%8F%E6%9F%AF%E5%85%8B%E6%96%AF%E4%BD%93&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="贝氏柯克斯体（页面不存在）">贝氏柯克斯体</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coxiella_burnetti" title="en:Coxiella burnetti"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Coxiella burnetti</span></a></span>）</span></span>有關，將胃中內容物誤吸到肺部容易造成<a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%AD%E6%B0%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="厭氧生物">厭氧生物</a>感染，<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%8A%E8%85%AB%E6%80%A7%E7%BA%96%E7%B6%AD%E5%8C%96" title="囊腫性纖維化">囊腫性纖維化</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E7%B6%A0%E8%86%BF%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="綠膿桿菌">綠膿桿菌</a>及金黃色葡萄球菌有關<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EBMED05_20-4"><a href="#cite_note-EBMED05-20">[20]</a></sup>。冬天較容易有<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E9%8F%88%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="肺炎鏈球菌">肺炎鏈球菌</a>，而且也需要考慮誤吸入大量<a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%AD%E6%B0%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="厭氧生物">厭氧生物</a>到肺部的可能性<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-5"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.97.85.E6.AF.92"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="病毒">病毒</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：病毒">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E" title="病毒性肺炎">病毒性肺炎</a></div>
<p>在成人身上，病毒性肺炎佔肺炎病例的三分之一，兒童則為15%<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-0"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup>。通常，較容易造成肺炎的病毒包含<a href="/wiki/%E9%BC%BB%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="鼻病毒">鼻病毒</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%86%A0%E7%8B%80%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="冠狀病毒">冠狀病毒</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E9%BB%8F%E6%B6%B2%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92%E7%A7%91" title="正黏液病毒科">正黏液病毒</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%BA%E9%A1%9E%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E9%81%93%E5%90%88%E8%83%9E%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="人類呼吸道合胞病毒">人類呼吸道合胞病毒</a>（RSV）、<a href="/wiki/%E8%85%BA%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="腺病毒">腺病毒</a>，以及<a href="/wiki/%E5%89%AF%E9%BB%8F%E6%B6%B2%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92%E7%A7%91" title="副黏液病毒科">副黏液病毒</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lancet11_11-7"><a href="#cite_note-Lancet11-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Viral09_36-0"><a href="#cite_note-Viral09-36">[36]</a></sup>。而<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B0%A1%E5%96%AE%E7%9A%B0%E7%96%B9%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="簡單皰疹病毒">簡單皰疹病毒</a>則鮮少造成肺炎，除了在某些特定族群像是新生兒、罹癌者、器官移植接受者，以及嚴重燒傷的病患身上才比較容易看到<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Text2010_37-0"><a href="#cite_note-Text2010-37">[37]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E5%99%A8%E5%AE%98%E7%A7%BB%E6%A4%8D" title="器官移植">器官移植</a>的病人或是<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E7%BC%BA%E9%99%B7" title="免疫缺陷">免疫缺陷</a>的病人若有罹患肺炎，很高機率是因為<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%A8%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="巨細胞病毒">巨細胞病毒</a>所引發的肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-1"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Text2010_37-1"><a href="#cite_note-Text2010-37">[37]</a></sup>。當人們受到病毒感染，可能會因為一些因素，像是身體免疫力較低下云云，造成他又感染了其他病菌，像是肺炎鏈球菌、金黃色葡萄球菌、流感嗜血桿菌等等，尤其是當在被病毒感染前便已有其他不健康狀況者，上述病菌感染更容易在病毒感染後連帶發生<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-6"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-2"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup>。
</p><p>不同的病毒種類在一年中不同時節會各有所主要佔據的時節，意思是可能一年中某個時期，某病毒種類較興盛，佔整體感染的比例較大，而另一個時期，則會換成另一種病毒種類佔的比例較大。舉例來說，在流感季節，流行感冒病毒感染所佔的總病毒感染比例可能可以達到一半以上<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-3"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup>。而有時候也會爆發其他種類病毒的感染，像是<a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%A2%E4%BB%96%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="漢他病毒">漢他病毒</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%86%A0%E7%8B%80%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="冠狀病毒">冠狀病毒</a>等<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-4"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.9C.9F.E8.8F.8C"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="真菌">真菌</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：真菌">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fungal pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="真菌型肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E5%9E%8B%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="真菌型肺炎（页面不存在）">真菌型肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fungal_pneumonia" title="en:Fungal pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fungal pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span></div>
<p>真菌性肺炎極為罕見，但在因為<a href="/wiki/%E8%89%BE%E6%BB%8B%E7%97%85" title="艾滋病">艾滋病</a>、服用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E6%8A%91%E5%88%B6%E8%8D%AF%E7%89%A9" title="免疫抑制药物">免疫抑制藥物</a>或是其他健康問題而導致的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="weakened immune systems" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="免疫功能較弱"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E5%8A%9F%E8%83%BD%E8%BC%83%E5%BC%B1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="免疫功能較弱（页面不存在）">免疫功能較弱</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/weakened_immune_systems" title="en:weakened immune systems"><span dir="auto" lang="en">weakened immune systems</span></a></span>）</span></span>的病人上會較常發生<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EBMED05_20-5"><a href="#cite_note-EBMED05-20">[20]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fungus2009_38-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fungus2009-38">[38]</a></sup> 。<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%9A%E8%86%9C%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87%E8%83%9E%E6%B5%86%E8%8F%8C" title="荚膜组织胞浆菌">莢膜組織胞漿菌</a>、芽生菌、<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E9%9A%B1%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="新型隱球菌">新型隱球菌</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E5%9B%8A%E8%9F%B2%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E" title="肺囊蟲肺炎">肺囊蟲肺炎</a>以及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B2%97%E7%90%83%E5%AD%A2%E5%AD%90%E8%8F%8C" title="粗球孢子菌">粗球孢子菌</a>等就是些常見的病原體。<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Histoplasmosis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="組織胞漿菌症"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B5%84%E7%B9%94%E8%83%9E%E6%BC%BF%E8%8F%8C%E7%97%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="組織胞漿菌症（页面不存在）">組織胞漿菌症</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Histoplasmosis" title="en:Histoplasmosis"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Histoplasmosis</span></a></span>）</span></span>好發於<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Mississippi embayment" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="密西西比河盆地"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3%E7%9B%86%E5%9C%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="密西西比河盆地（页面不存在）">密西西比河盆地</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mississippi_embayment" title="en:Mississippi embayment"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Mississippi embayment</span></a></span>）</span></span>，而<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Coccidioidomycosis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="球孢子菌症"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%90%83%E5%AD%A2%E5%AD%90%E8%8F%8C%E7%97%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="球孢子菌症（页面不存在）">球孢子菌症</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coccidioidomycosis" title="en:Coccidioidomycosis"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Coccidioidomycosis</span></a></span>）</span></span>則較常見於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8E%E5%9C%8B%E8%A5%BF%E5%8D%97%E6%96%B9" title="美國西南方">美國西南方</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EBMED05_20-6"><a href="#cite_note-EBMED05-20">[20]</a></sup> 。真菌性肺炎的病例數在20世紀後期因為人們旅遊活動變多以及免疫抑制藥物的使用增加而上升<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fungus2009_38-1"><a href="#cite_note-Fungus2009-38">[38]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AF.84.E7.94.9F.E8.9F.B2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="寄生蟲">寄生蟲</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：寄生蟲">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Parasitic pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="寄生蟲性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%84%E7%94%9F%E8%9F%B2%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="寄生蟲性肺炎（页面不存在）">寄生蟲性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parasitic_pneumonia" title="en:Parasitic pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Parasitic pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span></div>
<p>有許多<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%84%E7%94%9F%E8%99%AB" title="寄生虫">寄生蟲</a>也會感染肺臟，包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BC%93%E6%BC%BF%E8%9F%B2" title="弓漿蟲">弓漿蟲</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%B3%9E%E5%B0%8F%E6%A1%BF%E7%B7%9A%E8%9F%B2" title="糞小桿線蟲">糞小桿線蟲</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%9B%94%E8%9F%B2" title="蛔蟲">蛔蟲</a>，以及<a href="/wiki/%E7%98%A7%E5%8E%9F%E8%9F%B2" title="瘧原蟲">瘧原蟲</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M37_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-M37-39">[39]</a></sup>。這些寄生蟲通常經由皮膚接觸、食入，或病媒蚊叮咬而進入人體<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M37_39-1"><a href="#cite_note-M37-39">[39]</a></sup>。除了<a href="/wiki/%E8%A1%9B%E6%B0%8F%E8%82%BA%E5%90%B8%E8%9F%B2" title="衛氏肺吸蟲">衛氏肺吸蟲</a>之外，大部分的寄生蟲並不是直接傷害肺臟，而是先影響其他器官之後在直接或間接對肺部造成傷害<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M37_39-2"><a href="#cite_note-M37-39">[39]</a></sup>。有些寄生蟲，尤其是屬於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%9B%94%E8%99%AB%E5%B1%9E" title="蛔虫属">蛔蟲屬</a>和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Strongyloides" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="糞小桿線蟲屬"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B3%9E%E5%B0%8F%E6%A1%BF%E7%B7%9A%E8%9F%B2%E5%B1%AC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="糞小桿線蟲屬（页面不存在）">糞小桿線蟲屬</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Strongyloides" title="en:Strongyloides"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Strongyloides</span></a></span>）</span></span>的動物，會誘發強烈的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%97%9C%E9%85%B8%E6%80%A7%E7%90%83" title="嗜酸性球">嗜酸性球</a>活化反應，而這會導致<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Eosinophilic_pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="嗜酸性細胞肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%97%9C%E9%85%B8%E6%80%A7%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="嗜酸性細胞肺炎（页面不存在）">嗜酸性細胞肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eosinophilic_pneumonia" title="en:Eosinophilic pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Eosinophilic_pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M37_39-3"><a href="#cite_note-M37-39">[39]</a></sup>。在其他類別的感染中，如瘧疾等，會影響到肺的原因主要是因為細胞激素引發的全身性發炎所造成的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M37_39-4"><a href="#cite_note-M37-39">[39]</a></sup>。在<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B2%E9%96%8B%E7%99%BC%E5%9C%8B%E5%AE%B6" title="已開發國家">已開發國家</a>，寄生蟲感染最常出現在境外移入者<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M37_39-5"><a href="#cite_note-M37-39">[39]</a></sup>。綜觀全球，寄生蟲感染最常見是在免疫低下的人身上發生<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.89.B9.E7.99.BC.E6.80.A7.E8.82.BA.E7.82.8E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="特發性肺炎">特發性肺炎</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：特發性肺炎">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E7%99%BC%E6%80%A7%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E" title="特發性間質性肺炎">特發性間質性肺炎</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E7%99%BC%E6%80%A7%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E" title="特發性間質性肺炎">特發性間質性肺炎</a>或非感染性肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup>。是屬於<a href="/wiki/%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%97%85" title="間質性肺病">間質性肺病</a>這個類別。在這個類別中的疾病包含有<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Diffuse alveolar damage" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="瀰漫性肺泡傷害"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%80%B0%E6%BC%AB%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E6%B3%A1%E5%82%B7%E5%AE%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="瀰漫性肺泡傷害（页面不存在）">瀰漫性肺泡傷害</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Diffuse_alveolar_damage" title="en:Diffuse alveolar damage"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Diffuse alveolar damage</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Organizing pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="機化性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A9%9F%E5%8C%96%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="機化性肺炎（页面不存在）">機化性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Organizing_pneumonia" title="en:Organizing pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Organizing pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8D%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E" title="不特定的間質性肺炎">不特定的間質性肺炎</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="lymphocytic interstitial pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="淋巴性間質性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B7%8B%E5%B7%B4%E6%80%A7%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="淋巴性間質性肺炎（页面不存在）">淋巴性間質性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/lymphocytic_interstitial_pneumonia" title="en:lymphocytic interstitial pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">lymphocytic interstitial pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="desquamative interstitial pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="落屑性間質性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%90%BD%E5%B1%91%E6%80%A7%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="落屑性間質性肺炎（页面不存在）">落屑性間質性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/desquamative_interstitial_pneumonia" title="en:desquamative interstitial pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">desquamative interstitial pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="respiratory bronchiolitis interstitial lung disease" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="呼吸性細支氣管炎間質性肺病"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E6%80%A7%E7%B4%B0%E6%94%AF%E6%B0%A3%E7%AE%A1%E7%82%8E%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%97%85&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="呼吸性細支氣管炎間質性肺病（页面不存在）">呼吸性細支氣管炎間質性肺病</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/respiratory_bronchiolitis_interstitial_lung_disease" title="en:respiratory bronchiolitis interstitial lung disease"><span dir="auto" lang="en">respiratory bronchiolitis interstitial lung disease</span></a></span>）</span></span>，以及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="usual interstitial pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="常見型間質性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B8%B8%E8%A6%8B%E5%9E%8B%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="常見型間質性肺炎（页面不存在）">常見型間質性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/usual_interstitial_pneumonia" title="en:usual interstitial pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">usual interstitial pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.84.9F.E6.9F.93.E6.A9.9F.E5.88.B6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="感染機制">感染機制</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：感染機制">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:292px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:New_Pneumonia_cartoon.jpg"><img alt="A schematic diagram of the human lungs with an empty circle on the left representing a normal alveola and one on the right showing an alveola full of fluid as in pneumonia" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="611" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="354" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/New_Pneumonia_cartoon.jpg/290px-New_Pneumonia_cartoon.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/New_Pneumonia_cartoon.jpg/435px-New_Pneumonia_cartoon.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/fb/New_Pneumonia_cartoon.jpg 2x" width="290"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:New_Pneumonia_cartoon.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>肺炎的患者<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E6%B3%A1" title="肺泡">肺泡</a>內會充滿液體，導致氧合不良。圖左為正常肺泡，圖右則為肺炎的肺泡，圖中可看到肺泡腔內充滿液體</div></div></div>
<p>肺炎的進程通常始於<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8A%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E9%81%93%E6%84%9F%E6%9F%93" title="上呼吸道感染">上呼吸道感染</a>反應，之後才轉移感染下呼吸道<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PedNA09_43-0"><a href="#cite_note-PedNA09-43">[43]</a></sup>。肺炎的症狀除了肺組織發炎以外，也會造成<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Pulmonary consolidation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="肺實變"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E5%AF%A6%E8%AE%8A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="肺實變（页面不存在）">肺實變</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pulmonary_consolidation" title="en:Pulmonary consolidation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Pulmonary consolidation</span></a></span>）</span></span>，即<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E6%B3%A1" title="肺泡">肺泡</a>中充滿液體，進而阻擋血液氧合作用的現象<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dorlands_44-0"><a href="#cite_note-Dorlands-44">[44]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.97.85.E6.AF.92.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="病毒性">病毒性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：病毒性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>肺炎性的病毒可能藉由不同的管道進入肺部。呼吸道合胞病毒（RSV）通常是在病人觸摸到受感染的物體後，然後又碰觸眼、鼻而感染<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-5"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup> 。其他感染途徑則包含口鼻吸入空氣當中的飛沫而感染<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-7"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup> 。病毒感染上呼吸道之後，可能會再接著感染肺部，並入侵氣管內襯細胞、肺泡或是實質組織<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-6"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup>。另外如麻疹及皰疹病毒則是透過血液進入肺部<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gary2010_45-0"><a href="#cite_note-Gary2010-45">[45]</a></sup> 。肺部的病毒感染可能造成不同程度的細胞死亡<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-7"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup>，且一旦免疫系統開始對抗這些感染<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-8"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup>，以<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%96%AE%E6%A0%B8%E7%90%83" title="單核球">單核球</a>為主的<a href="/wiki/%E7%99%BD%E8%A1%80%E7%90%83" title="白血球">白血球</a>會啟動發炎反應<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gary2010_45-1"><a href="#cite_note-Gary2010-45">[45]</a></sup>，可能會對肺部形成更大的傷害<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M31_35-9"><a href="#cite_note-M31-35">[35]</a></sup>。在損傷肺部的同時，病毒也會同時影響其他<a href="/wiki/%E5%99%A8%E5%AE%98" title="器官">器官</a>，進一步阻礙正常的身體運作。病毒也會使得身體更易遭受其他細菌感染，因此病毒性肺炎有可能會<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%88%E4%BD%B5%E7%97%87" title="合併症">合併感染</a>細菌性肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Viral09_36-1"><a href="#cite_note-Viral09-36">[36]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.B4.B0.E8.8F.8C.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="細菌性">細菌性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：細菌性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>大多數的細菌能進入肺部主要是因為在呼吸時吸入寄宿在喉嚨或是鼻腔的微生物<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-8"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。有一半左右的人會於熟睡時吸入這些細菌<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M32_28-2"><a href="#cite_note-M32-28">[28]</a></sup>。人類的喉嚨時時充斥這些微生物，而那些有感染性的只會在特定時候與特定時機發難<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M32_28-3"><a href="#cite_note-M32-28">[28]</a></sup>。一些少數的細菌例如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B5%90%E6%A0%B8%E5%88%86%E6%9E%9D%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="結核分枝桿菌">結核分枝桿菌</a>還有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%80%80%E4%BC%8D%E8%BB%8D%E4%BA%BA%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="退伍軍人桿菌">退伍軍人桿菌</a>都是依靠飛沫到達肺部的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-9"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。而也有其他藉著血液傳播的病菌<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WHOPrevent2012_25-2"><a href="#cite_note-WHOPrevent2012-25">[25]</a></sup>。在細菌到達肺部後，會開始侵略在細胞以及肺泡間的空隙，在那裡，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%A8%E5%99%AC%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E" title="巨噬細胞">巨噬細胞</a>還有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%97%9C%E4%B8%AD%E6%80%A7%E7%90%83" title="嗜中性球">嗜中性球</a>（是種防疫性<a href="/wiki/%E7%99%BD%E8%A1%80%E7%90%83" title="白血球">白血球</a>）也會努力抵抗細菌的入侵<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup>。嗜中性球同時也釋出<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E6%BF%80%E7%B4%A0" title="細胞激素">細胞激素</a>，促進身體啟動免疫系統<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fein2006_47-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fein2006-47">[47]</a></sup> 。這會導致在細菌性肺炎中常見的發燒、寒顫與疲勞等症狀<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fein2006_47-1"><a href="#cite_note-Fein2006-47">[47]</a></sup> 。在血管周遭的嗜中性球、細菌以及細胞間液會充斥在肺泡內，這也是讓肺部在X光下會顯現出團狀陰影的原因<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E8.A8.BA.E6.96.B7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="診斷">診斷</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：診斷">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:PneumonisWedge09.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="3072" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/PneumonisWedge09.JPG/220px-PneumonisWedge09.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/PneumonisWedge09.JPG/330px-PneumonisWedge09.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/PneumonisWedge09.JPG/440px-PneumonisWedge09.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:PneumonisWedge09.JPG" title="放大"></a></div>醫師透過X光照射病患胸部，顯示右肺遭侵蝕產生空白（黑圈），才能診斷出肺炎。</div></div></div>
<table class="mbox-small listen noprint" style="border:1px solid #aaa;background-color:#f9f9f9">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" data-file-height="160" data-file-width="160" decoding="async" height="50" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/50px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/75px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/100px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png 2x" width="50"/></div></div></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><div class="haudio">
<div class="listen-file-header"><a href="/wiki/File:Crackles_pneumoniaO.ogg" title="File:Crackles pneumoniaO.ogg">Crackles</a></div>
<div><audio controls="" data-durationhint="14" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" data-mwtitle="Crackles_pneumoniaO.ogg" id="mwe_player_1" preload="none" style="width:232px;" width="232"><source data-bandwidth="46439" data-height="0" data-shorttitle="Ogg原始文件" data-title="原始Ogg文件 (46 kbps)" data-width="0" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/c7/Crackles_pneumoniaO.ogg" type='audio/ogg; codecs="vorbis"'/><source data-bandwidth="89200" data-height="0" data-shorttitle="MP3" data-title="MP3" data-transcodekey="mp3" data-width="0" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/c/c7/Crackles_pneumoniaO.ogg/Crackles_pneumoniaO.ogg.mp3" type="audio/mpeg"/><track data-dir="ltr" kind="subtitles" label="English‪（en）‬" src="https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/api.php?action=timedtext&amp;title=File%3ACrackles_pneumoniaO.ogg&amp;lang=en&amp;trackformat=vtt&amp;origin=%2A" srclang="en" type="text/vtt"/></audio></div>
<div class="description">Crackles heard in the lungs of a person with pneumonia using a stethoscope.</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td class="mbox-text" colspan="2"><hr/><i class="selfreference">播放此文件有问题？请参见<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%AA%92%E9%AB%94%E5%B9%AB%E5%8A%A9" title="Wikipedia:媒體幫助">媒體幫助</a>。</i></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>肺炎的診斷一般會配合身體體徵及<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%B8%E9%83%A8X%E5%85%89" title="胸部X光">胸部X光</a>進行<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diag10_49-0"><a href="#cite_note-Diag10-49">[49]</a></sup>。不過不容易確知其潛在的病因，因為沒有一個可以明確區分細菌性肺炎及非細菌性肺炎的標準<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lancet11_11-8"><a href="#cite_note-Lancet11-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diag10_49-1"><a href="#cite_note-Diag10-49">[49]</a></sup>。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C%E8%A1%9B%E7%94%9F%E7%B5%84%E7%B9%94" title="世界衛生組織">世界衛生組織</a>的資訊表示，兒童肺炎的臨床症狀可經由咳嗽、呼吸困難、呼吸急促、胸部凹陷及意識水平下降等症狀診斷<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WHOBook_50-0"><a href="#cite_note-WHOBook-50">[50]</a></sup>。呼吸急促的定義是二個月以下的兒童每分鐘呼吸超過60次，二個月到一歲的兒童每分鐘呼吸超過50次，一歲到五歲的兒童每分鐘呼吸超過40次<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WHOBook_50-1"><a href="#cite_note-WHOBook-50">[50]</a></sup>。對於兒童而言，呼吸急促及胸部凹陷對於肺炎的診斷比用<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%BD%E8%A8%BA%E5%99%A8" title="聽診器">聽診器</a>聽<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Crackles" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="碎裂聲"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A2%8E%E8%A3%82%E8%81%B2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="碎裂聲（页面不存在）">碎裂聲</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crackles" title="en:Crackles"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Crackles</span></a></span>）</span></span>呼吸音的靈敏度要高<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-4"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup>。對於五歲以下兒童而言，呼嚕聲（Grunting）及鼻翼搧動也可能是肺炎的症狀<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup>。
</p><p>一般對成人而言，輕微的肺炎不需要進一步的檢查<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BTS09_52-0"><a href="#cite_note-BTS09-52">[52]</a></sup>。若所有<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%BE%B5%E8%B1%A1" title="生命徵象">生命徵象</a>及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%83%B8%E8%85%94%E8%81%BD%E8%A8%BA" title="胸腔聽診">聽診</a>都正常，發生肺炎的風險很低<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup>。對於需要住院的病患而言，建議進行<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A1%80%E6%B0%A7%E9%A5%B1%E5%92%8C%E4%BB%AA" title="血氧饱和仪">血氧饱和仪</a>及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="chest radiography" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="胸腔放射線檢查"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%83%B8%E8%85%94%E6%94%BE%E5%B0%84%E7%B7%9A%E6%AA%A2%E6%9F%A5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="胸腔放射線檢查（页面不存在）">胸腔放射線檢查</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/chest_radiography" title="en:chest radiography"><span dir="auto" lang="en">chest radiography</span></a></span>）</span></span>，以及包括<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E8%A1%80%E7%BB%86%E8%83%9E%E8%AE%A1%E6%95%B0" title="全血细胞计数">全血细胞计数</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E8%A7%A3%E8%B4%A8" title="电解质">电解质</a>及<a href="/wiki/C%E5%8F%8D%E6%87%89%E8%9B%8B%E7%99%BD" title="C反應蛋白">C反應蛋白</a>在內的<a href="/wiki/%E8%A1%80%E6%B6%B2%E6%A3%80%E6%9F%A5" title="血液检查">血液检查</a>，可能也要進行<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%9D%E5%8A%9F%E8%83%BD%E6%B8%AC%E8%A9%A6" title="肝功能測試">肝功能測試</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BTS09_52-1"><a href="#cite_note-BTS09-52">[52]</a></sup>。<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="influenza-like illness" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="流感样疾病"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B5%81%E6%84%9F%E6%A0%B7%E7%96%BE%E7%97%85&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="流感样疾病（页面不存在）">流感样疾病</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/influenza-like_illness" title="en:influenza-like illness"><span dir="auto" lang="en">influenza-like illness</span></a></span>）</span></span>可以根據症状和体征進行的診斷，不過若要確認是否是罹患流感，需要進行檢查<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ILI05_54-0"><a href="#cite_note-ILI05-54">[54]</a></sup>。因此治療多半是根據此一群體是否出現流感，或是個人的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B5%81%E6%84%9F%E5%BF%AB%E9%80%9F%E8%AF%8A%E6%96%AD%E6%B5%8B%E8%AF%95" title="流感快速诊断测试">流感快速诊断测试</a>決定<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ILI05_54-1"><a href="#cite_note-ILI05-54">[54]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.90.86.E5.AD.B8.E6.AA.A2.E6.9F.A5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="理學檢查">理學檢查</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：理學檢查">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E7%90%86%E5%AD%B8%E6%AA%A2%E6%9F%A5" title="理學檢查">理學檢查</a>有時可發現患者有<a href="/wiki/%E4%BD%8E%E8%A1%80%E5%A3%93" title="低血壓">低血壓</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BF%83%E6%90%8F%E9%81%8E%E9%80%9F" title="心搏過速">心搏過速</a>，或<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Oxygenation (medical)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="血氧合"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A1%80%E6%B0%A7%E5%90%88&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="血氧合（页面不存在）">血氧飽和度</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oxygenation_(medical)" title="en:Oxygenation (medical)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Oxygenation (medical)</span></a></span>）</span></span>過低的症狀<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-10"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。在出現其他症狀前一至二天，患者可能出現呼吸速率大於正常值的症狀<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-11"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-M32_28-4"><a href="#cite_note-M32-28">[28]</a></sup>。患者的胸腔檢查結果可能正常，但是也可發現患病側胸腔擴張下降。經發炎的肺部從較大氣道傳來的粗糙呼吸音被稱為<a href="/wiki/%E6%94%AF%E6%B0%A3%E7%AE%A1" title="支氣管">支氣管</a>呼吸音，可使用<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%BD%E8%A8%BA%E5%99%A8" title="聽診器">聽診器</a><a href="/wiki/%E8%81%BD%E8%A8%BA" title="聽診">聽診</a>判斷<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-12"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>，在患者吸氣時可在感染區聽得碎裂聲（囉音）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-13"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。在患側<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Percussion (medicine)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="叩診"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%A9%E8%A8%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="叩診（页面不存在）">叩診</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Percussion_(medicine)" title="en:Percussion (medicine)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Percussion (medicine)</span></a></span>）</span></span>會呈現鈍音，且患者<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="vocal resonance" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="語聲共振"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AA%9E%E8%81%B2%E5%85%B1%E6%8C%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="語聲共振（页面不存在）">發音</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/vocal_resonance" title="en:vocal resonance"><span dir="auto" lang="en">vocal resonance</span></a></span>）</span></span>時的共振會較正常時增加，而<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="pleural effusion" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="肋膜腔積水"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%8B%E8%86%9C%E8%85%94%E7%A9%8D%E6%B0%B4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="肋膜腔積水（页面不存在）">肋膜腔積水</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pleural_effusion" title="en:pleural effusion"><span dir="auto" lang="en">pleural effusion</span></a></span>）</span></span>的共振則較正常時弱，藉此可以分辨兩種疾病<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BMJ06_8-3"><a href="#cite_note-BMJ06-8">[8]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.86.AB.E5.AD.B8.E5.BD.B1.E5.83.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="醫學影像">醫學影像</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：醫學影像">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RtPneuKidMark.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="859" data-file-width="875" decoding="async" height="216" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/RtPneuKidMark.png/220px-RtPneuKidMark.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/RtPneuKidMark.png/330px-RtPneuKidMark.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/RtPneuKidMark.png/440px-RtPneuKidMark.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:RtPneuKidMark.png" title="放大"></a></div>X光顯示兒童右中葉肺炎</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CT_scan_of_the_chest,_demonstrating_right-sided_pneumonia.jpg"><img alt="A black-and-white image shows the internal organs in cross-section as generated by CT. Where one would expect black on the left, one sees a whiter area with black sticks through it." class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2140" data-file-width="3006" decoding="async" height="157" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/CT_scan_of_the_chest%2C_demonstrating_right-sided_pneumonia.jpg/220px-CT_scan_of_the_chest%2C_demonstrating_right-sided_pneumonia.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/CT_scan_of_the_chest%2C_demonstrating_right-sided_pneumonia.jpg/330px-CT_scan_of_the_chest%2C_demonstrating_right-sided_pneumonia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/CT_scan_of_the_chest%2C_demonstrating_right-sided_pneumonia.jpg/440px-CT_scan_of_the_chest%2C_demonstrating_right-sided_pneumonia.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:CT_scan_of_the_chest,_demonstrating_right-sided_pneumonia.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>胸部 CT 顯示右側肺炎（圖像左側）</div></div></div>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="chest radiograph" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="胸腔照影"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%83%B8%E8%85%94%E7%85%A7%E5%BD%B1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="胸腔照影（页面不存在）">胸部X光照片</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/chest_radiograph" title="en:chest radiograph"><span dir="auto" lang="en">chest radiograph</span></a></span>）</span></span>常被拿來用作診斷的依據之一<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-5"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup>。當病症輕微，通常不會照胸部X光片，除非像是：有產生潛在併發症的可能性、治療後未改善，或是原因不明者<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-6"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BTS09_52-2"><a href="#cite_note-BTS09-52">[52]</a></sup>。若是病人已經嚴重到需要住院時，則建議要照胸部X光片<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BTS09_52-3"><a href="#cite_note-BTS09-52">[52]</a></sup>。但是要澄清的是，X光片所顯現出來的結果不一定能完全呈現病人病症之嚴重程度，而且X光片沒辦法區分到底此肺炎是細菌或是病毒感染<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-7"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup>。
</p><p>由X光片來看，肺炎可以分類為<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="lobar pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="大葉性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%A7%E8%91%89%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="大葉性肺炎（页面不存在）">大葉性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/lobar_pneumonia" title="en:lobar pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">lobar pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、支氣管肺炎（有時也會稱為小葉性肺炎）及<a href="/wiki/%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%97%85" title="間質性肺病">間質性肺病</a>。細菌感染的社區性肺炎典型症狀有一個<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="lung segmental lobe" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="肺葉節段"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E8%91%89%E7%AF%80%E6%AE%B5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="肺葉節段（页面不存在）">肺葉節段</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/lung_segmental_lobe" title="en:lung segmental lobe"><span dir="auto" lang="en">lung segmental lobe</span></a></span>）</span></span>的肺實變，稱為大葉性肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-2"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup>。然而並非所有的細菌性肺炎皆為大葉性肺炎，也並非所有的大葉性肺炎皆由細菌所引起，其他肺炎也會有類似的情形<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-3"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup>。吸入性肺炎的特點是肺兩側底部及右肺葉呈現混濁<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-4"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup>。病毒性肺炎的X光片可能是正常的，也可能有過度充氣、兩側大片浸潤、或是類似細菌性肺炎的肺實變情形<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-5"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup>。肺炎在早期時可能無法從X光片上看出來，特別是在脫水的情況下，若有<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%A5%E8%83%96%E7%97%87" title="肥胖症">肥胖症</a>其他肺部病史，也不易判斷<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Clinic2011_24-14"><a href="#cite_note-Clinic2011-24">[24]</a></sup>。有些情形，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/X%E5%B0%84%E7%BA%BF%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%BA%E6%96%AD%E5%B1%82%E6%88%90%E5%83%8F" title="X射线计算机断层成像">X射线计算机断层成像</a>可以看出一些進一步的資訊<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-6"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.BE.AE.E7.94.9F.E7.89.A9.E5.AD.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="微生物學">微生物學</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：微生物學">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>倘若發病病患的管理止於社區範圍，那去探究發病原並不具備成本效益，且基本上對於疾病管控的影響微乎其微<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Develop11_22-8"><a href="#cite_note-Develop11-22">[22]</a></sup>。針對治療沒有效果的患者，該考慮進行<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="sputum culture" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="痰液培養"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%97%B0%E6%B6%B2%E5%9F%B9%E9%A4%8A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="痰液培養（页面不存在）">痰液培養</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/sputum_culture" title="en:sputum culture"><span dir="auto" lang="en">sputum culture</span></a></span>）</span></span>，而有慢性咳痰困擾的患者則應進行<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B5%90%E6%A0%B8%E5%88%86%E6%94%AF%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="結核分支桿菌">結核分支桿菌</a>的培養<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BTS09_52-4"><a href="#cite_note-BTS09-52">[52]</a></sup>。在公共衛生考量的前提下，在疫情爆發時，會針對特定的病原體進行篩檢作業<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BTS09_52-5"><a href="#cite_note-BTS09-52">[52]</a></sup>。對於嚴重肺炎的住院患者，建議同時進行痰液和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="blood cultures" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="血液培養"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A1%80%E6%B6%B2%E5%9F%B9%E9%A4%8A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="血液培養（页面不存在）">血液培養</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/blood_cultures" title="en:blood cultures"><span dir="auto" lang="en">blood cultures</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BTS09_52-6"><a href="#cite_note-BTS09-52">[52]</a></sup>，也要驗驗尿液是否有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BB%8D%E5%9C%98%E8%8F%8C" title="軍團菌">退伍軍人菌</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%8F%88%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="鏈球菌">鏈球菌</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%97%E5%8E%9F" title="抗原">抗原</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IDSA2007_56-0"><a href="#cite_note-IDSA2007-56">[56]</a></sup>。若利用病毒培養、<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%9A%E5%90%88%E9%85%B6%E9%93%BE%E5%BC%8F%E5%8F%8D%E5%BA%94" title="聚合酶链式反应">聚合酶链式反应</a>（PCR）或其他方式，偵測到病毒或是其抗原，即可確認是病毒感染<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lancet11_11-9"><a href="#cite_note-Lancet11-11">[11]</a></sup>。在常規的微生物檢查中，只有15%能找到可疑的致病原<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BMJ06_8-4"><a href="#cite_note-BMJ06-8">[8]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.91.91.E5.88.A5.E8.A8.BA.E6.96.B7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="鑑別診斷">鑑別診斷</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：鑑別診斷">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>有許多疾病的症狀與表現與肺炎相近，包括：<a href="/wiki/%E6%85%A2%E6%80%A7%E9%98%BB%E5%A1%9E%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%97%85" title="慢性阻塞性肺病">慢性阻塞性肺病</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%93%AE%E5%96%98" title="哮喘">哮喘</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E6%B0%B4%E8%85%AB" title="肺水腫">肺水腫</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%94%AF%E6%B0%A3%E7%AE%A1%E6%93%B4%E5%BC%B5" title="支氣管擴張">支氣管擴張</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%99%8C" title="肺癌">肺癌</a>、以及<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E6%A0%93%E5%A1%9E" title="肺栓塞">肺栓塞</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BMJ06_8-5"><a href="#cite_note-BMJ06-8">[8]</a></sup> 。哮喘與慢性阻塞性肺病通常伴隨著<a href="/wiki/%E5%96%98%E9%B3%B4" title="喘鳴">喘鳴</a>聲，這個症狀在肺炎較為少見，而肺水腫的患者通常會有異常的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BF%83%E9%9B%BB%E5%9C%96" title="心電圖">心電圖</a>。癌症與支氣管擴張症造成的咳嗽通常持續較長時間。肺栓塞通常會伴隨著急性發作的胸痛與<a href="/wiki/%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E5%9B%B0%E9%9A%BE" title="呼吸困难">呼吸困難</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BMJ06_8-6"><a href="#cite_note-BMJ06-8">[8]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.88.86.E9.A1.9E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="分類">分類</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：分類">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Classification_of_pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="肺炎的分類"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E7%9A%84%E5%88%86%E9%A1%9E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="肺炎的分類（页面不存在）">肺炎的分類</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classification_of_pneumonia" title="en:Classification of pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Classification_of_pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span></div>
<p>肺炎最常依感染原因或地點來分類：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Community-acquired_pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Community-acquired_pneumonia"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Community-acquired_pneumonia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Community-acquired pneumonia（页面不存在）">社區性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Community-acquired_pneumonia" title="en:Community-acquired pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Community-acquired_pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Healthcare-associated_pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Healthcare-associated_pneumonia"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Healthcare-associated_pneumonia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Healthcare-associated pneumonia（页面不存在）">醫療照護相關肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Healthcare-associated_pneumonia" title="en:Healthcare-associated pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Healthcare-associated_pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Hospital-acquired_pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Hospital-acquired_pneumonia"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Hospital-acquired_pneumonia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Hospital-acquired pneumonia（页面不存在）">院內感染性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hospital-acquired_pneumonia" title="en:Hospital-acquired pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Hospital-acquired_pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Aspiration_pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Aspiration_pneumonia"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Aspiration_pneumonia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Aspiration pneumonia（页面不存在）">吸入性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aspiration_pneumonia" title="en:Aspiration pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Aspiration_pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、以及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="ventilator-associated pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="ventilator-associated pneumonia"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ventilator-associated_pneumonia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ventilator-associated pneumonia（页面不存在）">呼吸器相關肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ventilator-associated_pneumonia" title="en:ventilator-associated pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">ventilator-associated pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-7"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup>。另外，也可以以感染波及的範圍來分類：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="lobar pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="大葉性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%A7%E8%91%89%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="大葉性肺炎（页面不存在）">大葉性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/lobar_pneumonia" title="en:lobar pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">lobar pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%94%AF%E6%B0%A3%E7%AE%A1%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E" title="支氣管肺炎">支氣管肺炎</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%80%A5%E6%80%A7%E9%96%93%E8%B3%AA%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E" title="急性間質性肺炎">急性間質性肺炎</a>等<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rad07_33-8"><a href="#cite_note-Rad07-33">[33]</a></sup>。以肺炎的致病菌來分類也是另一個常見的方式<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup>。兒童的肺炎有時也可以用症狀嚴重程度來分類：非嚴重、嚴重、極嚴重<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup>。
</p><p>發生肺炎的地點在治療上是很重要的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid_19199181_59-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid_19199181-59">[59]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid_15699079_60-0"><a href="#cite_note-pmid_15699079-60">[60]</a></sup>，它可以提供許多資訊，包括：可能的致病菌種類<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid_19199181_59-1"><a href="#cite_note-pmid_19199181-59">[59]</a></sup>、可能的感染原因、可能有效的抗生素種類<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid_19199181_59-2"><a href="#cite_note-pmid_19199181-59">[59]</a></sup>，考慮患者的健康狀況，還可以推估可能發生的併發症。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.A4.BE.E5.8D.80.E6.80.A7.E8.82.BA.E7.82.8E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="社區性肺炎">社區性肺炎</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="编辑章节：社區性肺炎">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Community-acquired pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="社區性肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A4%BE%E5%8D%80%E6%80%A7%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="社區性肺炎（页面不存在）">社區性肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Community-acquired_pneumonia" title="en:Community-acquired pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Community-acquired pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span></div>
<p>社區性肺炎（CAP）是在一般社區感染而非醫療機構中的肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid_19199181_59-3"><a href="#cite_note-pmid_19199181-59">[59]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid_15699079_60-1"><a href="#cite_note-pmid_15699079-60">[60]</a></sup>，比起醫療照護相關肺炎，多重抗藥性菌引發的社區性肺炎的比例相對較低，即使近來抗藥性菌在社區性肺炎已不再少見，比起醫療照護相關肺炎來說還是相對來得少。社區型肺炎在各國的感染症死因排名中都名列前茅<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup>。85%的社區型肺炎的致病體是典型的細菌，包括了<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E9%8F%88%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="肺炎鏈球菌">肺炎鏈球菌</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%81%E6%84%9F%E5%97%9C%E8%A1%80%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="流感嗜血桿菌">流感嗜血桿菌</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Moraxella catarrhalis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="卡他莫拉菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%A1%E4%BB%96%E8%8E%AB%E6%8B%89%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="卡他莫拉菌（页面不存在）">卡他莫拉菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moraxella_catarrhalis" title="en:Moraxella catarrhalis"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Moraxella catarrhalis</span></a></span>）</span></span>（<i>Moraxella catarrhalis</i>）。剩下的15%則由所謂的非典型致病體造成，包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E5%88%86%E6%9E%9D%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="肺炎分枝桿菌">肺炎分枝桿菌</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Chlamydia pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="肺炎衣原體"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E%E8%A1%A3%E5%8E%9F%E9%AB%94&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="肺炎衣原體（页面不存在）">肺炎衣原體</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chlamydia_pneumonia" title="en:Chlamydia pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Chlamydia pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>（<i>Chlamydia pneumonia</i>）、和<a href="/wiki/%E8%BB%8D%E5%9C%98%E8%8F%8C%E5%B1%AC" title="軍團菌屬">退伍軍人菌屬</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup>。一般而言，如<a href="/wiki/%E7%B6%A0%E8%86%BF%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="綠膿桿菌">綠膿桿菌</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%94%BE%E7%BA%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="放线菌">放線菌</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%85%B8%E6%A1%BF%E8%8F%8C" title="腸桿菌">腸桿菌</a>等需氧的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%A9%E5%85%B0%E6%B0%8F%E9%98%B4%E6%80%A7%E8%8F%8C" title="革兰氏阴性菌">革蘭氏陰性桿菌</a>較少造成社區型肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup>。
</p><p><br/>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.91.BC.E5.90.B8.E5.99.A8.E7.9B.B8.E9.97.9C.E8.82.BA.E7.82.8E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="呼吸器相關肺炎">呼吸器相關肺炎</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="编辑章节：呼吸器相關肺炎">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ventilatior-associated pneumonia" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="呼吸器相關肺炎"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E5%99%A8%E7%9B%B8%E9%97%9C%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="呼吸器相關肺炎（页面不存在）">呼吸器相關肺炎</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ventilatior-associated_pneumonia" title="en:Ventilatior-associated pneumonia"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ventilatior-associated pneumonia</span></a></span>）</span></span>指的是發生在使用<span class="ilh-all ilh-blue" data-foreign-title="mechanical ventilation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="呼吸器"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E5%91%BC%E5%90%B8%E5%99%A8" title="呼吸器">呼吸器</a></span></span>的患者身上的肺部感染<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid_19199181_59-4"><a href="#cite_note-pmid_19199181-59">[59]</a></sup>，嚴格的定義是在進行氣管內管插管後超過48至72小時後發生的肺炎<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pmid_15699079_60-2"><a href="#cite_note-pmid_15699079-60">[60]</a></sup>。呼吸器正如同其他的醫療器材有一定的感染風險，原因是其內部零件與表面容易有細菌群聚，即使在規律清潔的狀況下也難以避免。依賴呼吸器的患者通常原先狀況就已不佳，一旦發生肺炎通常不容易處理。<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E7%BC%BA%E9%99%B7" title="免疫缺陷">免疫機能不全</a>發生的原因通常包含營養狀況不佳，或患有其他合併症等等。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.99.A2.E5.85.A7.E6.84.9F.E6.9F.93.E6.80.A7.E8.82.BA.E7.82.8E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="院內感染性肺炎">院內感染性肺炎</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%82%BA%E7%82%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="编辑章节：院內感染性肺炎">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
